 ' aap kitni achchheekar drive karte hanis baat kaa andaja is baat se lagata he ki aap car ko kitni jaldi or kitne behatar tareeke se park karte hai
 Of course this is the hallmark of a good driver, but we also need to pay attention to some precautions before standing the car on busy roads and parking areas
 1)car park karne se pehle yah jarur jaanch len ki vah jagah parking ke liye he bhi yaa nahin
 2) Take special care of No Standing Zone, No Parking Zone
 3)kabhi car ko kisi get ke saamne park nahin karen
 4) Avoid parking the car even in crowded areas such as bus stops, post boxes, taxis or rickshaw stands
 5)kisi ped ke neeche gaadi park naa hi karen to behatar he
 6) Parking a car under a tree can protect your car from sunlight during the day, but in the event of twigs falling or thunderstorms, the tree may suffer more damage
 7)ped ke neeche car park karne par pakshiyon ke mel-mutr bhi aapaki gaadi ke paint ko kharaab kar sakate hai
 8) Learn the right way to use hand brake
 9)aam taur par log car park kar use giyar main daal dete hai or hand brake laga dete hai
 Do not do this
 aisi sthiti adhiktam bhaar giyar par hota he na ki hand brake par
 10) While parking the car in hilly areas, use the hand brake
 11)bageeche ke nikat gaadi park kerani pade to hand brake jarur lagaaein
 12) It would be better to put the car in neutral gear and apply hand brake
 13)hand brake kaa istemaal karte vakt uske push batan ko jarur dabaaen
 14) If you are standing next to the wall, then keep a distance from the wall
 15)car park karte vakt koi rasta block naa karen

 guds and services tex 1 july se lagu ho chukaa he
 There are many such provisions in this new tax system which are believed by the experts that due to these, once the Inspector Raj can be started in the country
 jiesti kanoon main kaarobaari ko munafkhori or tex asangati ke chalate giraftaar karne ke praavdhaan ke chalate mana rahaa he ki iske chalate tex vibhaag ke karmchaariyon ko kaarobaari ke thikaanon par inspection, chhapemari or jabti karne kaa vishesh adhikaar mil jayega
 These provisions will give unlimited powers to field officers of the tax department for businessmen in the country
 sijisti or esgstike karmchaaree kisi bhi kaarobaari yaa transporter yaa warehouse par inspection or chhapemari mahaj is shaq par kar sakate hai ki ukt jadah par tex chori kii ja rahi he yaa kii jane kii sambhaavna he
 At the same time, in Clause 171, GST has been provided that companies will get the benefit of input tax credit by providing cheap products to customers
 is niyam ke tahat yah jaruri ho jaataa he ki jiesti dhaanche ke samanaantar ek dhaancha khadaa kiya jaae jisase companiyon kii munafkhori par kadi najar rakhi ja sake
 In addition, tax experts on the provisions of GST believe that the tax rates of 5,12, 18 and 28 per cent could lead to new differences between the business and the tax department
 jiesti ke daayre se bachane ke liye jahaan kaarobaariyon kii koshish apane product kaa aankalan inamen se nunatam daayre main karaane kii hogi
 At the same time, in order to collect more tax, the tax department will try to subject most products to a larger scope
 lihaaja, aisi sthiti main kaarobaari or tex vibhaag main matbhed badhane ke asaar rahenge or inke niptaare ke liye tex tribunel kii bhoomika ahm ho jaaegi
 Under GST, there is a provision for any businessman to go to jail if he is caught for stealing tax or committing fraud
 praavdhaan ke mutabik yadi kendra or rajya kii tex sanstha main kisi kamishnar str ke aadhikari ke paas kisi kaarobaari par tex chori main lipt hone kaa paryaapt kaaran he to vah uski giraftaar kaa aadesh de saktaa he

 Let us know the diseases caused by sitting cross legs
 
 
 1
 Increased blood pressure: In many studies, it has been proved that sitting with legs crossed for a long time increases blood pressure to a great extent
 isliye health export blad pressure ke shikaar logon ke saath aise logon ko bhi is posture main baithne se bachane kii hidaayat dete hai jinhen blad pressure kii pareshaani nahin he
 2
 nerve paralisis kaa khatra:agar aap zyada samay tak pairon ko cross karke baithte ho to isse aapke pairon kii nason ko nuksaan pahunch saktaa he
 Because the pressure on the veins of the feet increases due to sitting, due to which there is a risk of damage to the veins
 itnaa hi nahin balki is posture main baithne se vyaktiperonol nerve paralisiskaa shikaar bhi ho saktaa he
 3
 bald sarculation bigadanaa:ek pair ko duusare pair par rakhkar baithne ke kaaran dil main zyada blad pahunchataa he
 Because when you sit with your legs crossed, the blood stops coming from the top down and Hart starts pumping upside down
 jis vajah se sharir main blad sarculation bighad jaataa he
 4
 spidar wain kaa khatra:zyada samay tak ek pair ko duusare pair par rakhkar baithne se aap spidar wain ke shikaar ho sakate hai
 Because by putting one foot on the other foot, the blood reaching the feet stops circulating in the heart itself
